permB_basc_desB_suc

Permutaion of type B, $\pi(0)=0$, in words, with $basc$, $des_B$, $suc$ (back to Data page)

定義：

  • Permutaion of type B：

  • $basc$($\rho$) = # $\{i \mid \rho(i) < \rho(i+1)-1 \}$

  • $des_B$($\rho$) = # $\{i \mid \rho(i) > \rho(i+1) \}$

  • $suc$($\rho$) = # $\{i \mid \rho(i) = \rho(i+1) -1 \}$

exc, aexc, fix

  • 總數
  • 分項
  • Data
